<p><b>Aulsondro "Novelist" Hamilton</b>, better known by his stage name <b>Emcee N.I.C.E.</b>, is an American <a href="/wiki/Christian_hip_hop" title="Christian hip hop">Christian hip hop</a> recording artist.<a href="/wiki/Rapper" class="mw-redirect" title="Rapper">rapper</a>, singer, songwriter, record and <a href="/wiki/Film_producer" title="Film producer">film producer</a>, record executive, actor, an American Inventor and a Entrepreneur and former lead vocalist/rapper of the duo <a href="/wiki/KansasCali" title="KansasCali">KansasCali</a>.
He is the co-creator of the animated music series <a href="/wiki/Da_Jammies" title="Da Jammies">Da Jammies</a>, The co-founder of The Stellar Award winning radio station <a href="/wiki/God%27s_House_of_Hip_Hop_Radio" title="God&#39;s House of Hip Hop Radio">God’s House of Hip Hop Radio</a><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> powered by <a href="/wiki/Dash_Radio" title="Dash Radio">Dash Radio</a>, A Best Selling Author for his book “Music Release University”.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-rapzilla.com_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rapzilla.com-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> He is president of two non-profit organizations, The iTL Foundation (Information, Technology &amp; Literacy) of Los Angeles <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> and Urbanomics 101,<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> the Managing Editor for RYZE Magazine,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> a christian hip hop lifestyle magazine and an American Inventor.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> He is the co-producer of 2 Pac's <a href="/wiki/Thugz_Mansion" title="Thugz Mansion">Thugz Mansion</a> acoustic, the first single released from the certified triple platinum album <a href="/wiki/Better_Dayz" title="Better Dayz">Better Dayz</a> and the Nas acoustic <a href="/wiki/Thugz_Mansion" title="Thugz Mansion">Thugz Mansion (N.Y.)</a>, off of the certified platinum album <a href="/wiki/God%27s_Son_(album)" title="God&#39;s Son (album)">God's Son</a>
</p><p>Emcee N.I.C.E.’s debut recording as a Christian Hip Hop Recording artist came when the album <a href="/wiki/Praise" title="Praise">Praise</a> was released in 2017 and became his first solo project to reach No. 1 on the <a href="/wiki/Billboard_Charts" class="mw-redirect" title="Billboard Charts">Billboard Top Gospel Albums</a> and “Billboard Gospel Album Sales” the album would yield Five No. 1 hit records on the <i>Billboard</i> charts in "I Got Angels"<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> claiming two positions along with "Glory to God" (ft. Fred Hammond)<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> &amp; <a href="/wiki/MRC_Data" class="mw-redirect" title="MRC Data">Nielsen BDS</a> including a No. 1 <a href="/wiki/Gospel_music" title="Gospel music">gospel</a> album in <i><a href="/wiki/Praise_(album)" title="Praise (album)">Praise</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Emcee N.I.C.E. received nominations for Rap Hip-Hop Gospel CD of the Year and Gospel Hip Hop Radio Station of Year at the <a href="/wiki/34th_Annual_Stellar_Awards" title="34th Annual Stellar Awards">34th</a> <a href="/wiki/Stellar_Awards" title="Stellar Awards">Annual Stellar Awards</a>, the last of which he won. He is also a 12 time "The Gospel Spin Awards" winner, in the categories of "Internet Radio Personality of the Year," 2 time "Best Radio Show 2 or More – (God's Calamari w/ Emcee N.I.C.E. &amp; The God Squad)," 2 time "Voice of the Year, Station Manager/Program Director of the Year" are the notables, he received a total of 17 Nominations in Gospel radio from the Gospel Spin Award and in 2021 Emcee N.I.C.E. was honored as "Radio Man of the Year."<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2023)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>Emcee N.I.C.E. also known as Novelist with the duo KansasCali, has been on six motion picture soundtracks, Oscar Award Winning film <a href="/wiki/Crash_(2004_film)" title="Crash (2004 film)">Crash</a> song "If I...", Mr. &amp; Mrs. Smith (International Soundtrack)<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> song "If I Never See You Again", <a href="/wiki/Haven_(soundtrack)" title="Haven (soundtrack)">Haven Original Soundtrack</a> song "Uuuh", <a href="/wiki/Kickin%27_It_Old_Skool" title="Kickin&#39; It Old Skool">Kickin' It Old Skool</a><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> song "The Life", <a href="/wiki/Once_in_a_Lifetime:_The_Extraordinary_Story_of_the_New_York_Cosmos" title="Once in a Lifetime: The Extraordinary Story of the New York Cosmos">Once in a Lifetime: The Extraordinary Story of the New York Cosmos</a> song "U Gotta Fight!"
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Emcee_N.I.C.E.&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1097763485"><table class="box-Expand_section plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg" class="mw-file-description"><img alt="[icon]" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="14" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="44" data-file-height="31" /></a></span></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs expansion</b>. You can help by <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Emcee_N.I.C.E.&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">adding to it</a>.  <span class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">March 2023</span>)</i></span></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>In 2015, under his real name Aulsondro Hamilton, he <a href="/wiki/Voice_actor" class="mw-redirect" title="Voice actor">voiced</a> the character "Novelist" in a 3D animated music series entitled <a href="/wiki/Da_Jammies" title="Da Jammies">Da Jammies</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Music_Videos">Music Videos</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Emcee_N.I.C.E.&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Music Videos">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A music video for "Thugz Mansion" was shot. The video was nominated at the 2003 <a href="/wiki/MTV_Video_Music_Awards" title="MTV Video Music Awards">MTV Video Music Awards</a> for Best Rap Video.
</p>
<ul><li>other music videos includes:</li>
<li>"If U Wanna Groove" with <a href="/wiki/Lighter_Shade_of_Brown" class="mw-redirect" title="Lighter Shade of Brown">Lighter Shade of Brown</a></li>
<li>"If I..." with <a href="/wiki/KansasCali" title="KansasCali">KansasCali</a></li>
<li>"The Life" with <a href="/wiki/KansasCali" title="KansasCali">KansasCali</a></li>
<li>"Life of The Party" with <a href="/wiki/Stacey_Dash" title="Stacey Dash">Stacey Dash</a> &amp; Blake Smith</li>
<li>"I Got Angels"</li>
<li>"This Is TBL" with Lamontt Blackshire &amp; DaLomonze</li>
<li>"Precious Stones" with Bryann Trejo</li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Books">Books</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Emcee_N.I.C.E.&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Books">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
